module dataMem(input[10:0] currentState,
input[11:0] stateIp1,stateIp2,stateIp3,
input [29:0] complexInput1,RealInput1,complexInput2,RealInput2,complexInput3,RealInput3,
output reg [29:0] complexOut1,complexOut2,realOut1,realOut2,twiddleFactorReal,twiddleFactorComplx,
output reg [11:0] stateOp1,stateOp2,
output reg outputFlag,
input[11:0] outputAddress,
output reg [29:0] complexOutput,realOutput);

//		     ---------------------------
//from counter 	--> |state  		  	|-->
//		--> |ReIp1  		  ReOp1	|-->
//		--> |ReIp2   		  ReOp2	|-->
//		--> |ReIp3 		  	|-->
//		--> |CmpIp1		 CmpOp1	|-->
//		--> |CmpIp2		 CmpOp2	|-->
//		--> |CmpIp3		 	|-->
//		--> |state1	     TwiddleRe  |-->
//		--> |state2       TwiddleCmplxOp|-->
//		--> |state3	        pushout	|-->
//		--> |currentstate    		|<--
//		    |			 state1	|-->
//		    |			 state2	|-->
//		     -----------^-------o-------
//				|	|                
//			      clock   reset

reg [29:0] complxMem[0:2303],realMem[0:2303];
always @(*) begin
	// output transfer begin
		if((stateIp2+256)>12'd2048) begin
		outputFlag<=1'b1;
		end
		complexOutput<=complxMem[outputAddress];
		realOutput<=realMem[outputAddress];
		realMem[stateIp1]<=RealInput1;
		realMem[stateIp2]<=RealInput2;
		realMem[stateIp3]<=RealInput3;
		complxMem[stateIp1]<=complexInput1;
		complxMem[stateIp2]<=complexInput2;
		complxMem[stateIp3]<=complexInput3;
		case (currentState)
			 0: begin
				 complexOut1 <= 30'd0;
				 realOut1 <= 30'd0;
				 complexOut2 <= 30'd0;
				 realOut2 <= 30'd0;
				 twiddleFactorReal <=30'd0;
				 twiddleFactorComplx <=30'd0;
				 stateOp1<=11'd0;
				 stateOp2<=11'd0;
		outputFlag<=1'b0;
			 end
			 default: begin
				 complexOut1 = 30'dx;
				 realOut1 = 30'dx;
				 complexOut2 = 30'dx;
				 realOut2 = 30'dx;
				 twiddleFactorReal =30'dx;
				 twiddleFactorComplx =30'dx;
			 end
			 11'd1 : begin
				 //(0,128)
				 complexOut1 = complxMem[0];
				 realOut1 = realMem[0];
				 complexOut2 = complxMem[128];
				 realOut2 = realMem[128];
				 twiddleFactorReal =1048576.0;
				 twiddleFactorComplx =-0.0;
				 stateOp1<=12'd256;
				 stateOp2<=12'd384;
			 end
			 11'd2 : begin
				 //(1,129)
				 complexOut1 = complxMem[1];
				 realOut1 = realMem[1];
				 complexOut2 = complxMem[129];
				 realOut2 = realMem[129];
				 twiddleFactorReal =1048576.0;
				 twiddleFactorComplx =-0.0;
				 stateOp1<=12'd257;
				 stateOp2<=12'd385;
			 end

				 realOut2 = realMem[130];
				 twiddleFactorReal =1048576.0;

				 stateOp1<=12'd258;

				 realOut2 = realMem[131];
